Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go too deep, for otherwise the swelling would turn purple, and perform the cauterization according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Apres make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the scrotum; and let the cauterization be long, one above the knee and the other below, across the leg; and leave the cauterizations in place for a long time without treating them, so that they heal; after this treat the other injuries as we have said.
de la menoison	of the castle
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the stomach pain comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive fluids that are in the stomach and intestines remain unafected, it cannot be treated with any remedies; and you will see the patient suffer greatly and become very weak, so make a large cauterization around the navel according to what he has spoken of before, or a cauterization of the navel; and four cauterizations around the loins, one above and one below, near the sinews, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abundant and the patient suffering, make a fire cautery on his hand, and a cautery on each finger, and two small cauterizations on the stomach, because the cure is profitable when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the cure for hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are at the foundation, one or more, and are old and have big cold and moist sores that are corrupt, and are cured as we have said in the divisions, and it does not profit if you make fire: III on the spine of the back, which is all outside with oil little by little and squaring, and I cauterize outside the two bones; and if you think that his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and we see swell the face, then let the face have a big cautery, as it is said before, and another on the liver, and another on the bolea to all cauterize nailed; and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating, let the wound remain healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the pus which is called “thelu”
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When coping with the pus, if you heat the cautery which seems like a razor, and then set it all ablaze on top of the coped pus; and leave it so that the cautery comes to the birth of the vein, from which it will come out; do this once or twice, and if there is much pus, cauterize each one as we have said; after treating with beneficial oils as long as they remain healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery on top of the pustule, it will provide more help.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot tolerate surgery or opening, which we will describe in its place, if there comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If there is no opening in the vein, and it is swollen and filled with pus and corruption, then you must provide the whole tent of suture, and be careful that you know exactly how much of the tent it needs.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cautery that seems like a razor, pour it into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent has entered, and restart the cautery as many times as there is corruption and pus to be burned, once or twice, according to the amount of medicine needed; and beware of the nerves that are injured, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the core of the bladder and intestine, beware of these vessels, and do not make a cut except in the middle, and think that it is not useless; after having healed the vessel as long as it is healthy, and if the vessels are broken, and the bones are exposed for a long time, then know that the vessel is completely healed; and if the bones are not exposed, know that the vessel is three-quarters healed, and the bone at the bottom is corrupt. And thus, as one of these that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain of the kidneys comes with a strong wind and does not respond to the treatment of women, then you should make a cautery on the kidneys from both sides with the clavicle cautery that we have mentioned before; and if we do this in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and it will be more effective.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak from pain and moisture, so that the patient retenes urine, then you make a cautery on the bladder's upper part from behind, where the hair of the perineum begins, and one on each side, and each as long as a finger; and you make another cautery behind, where it is necessary; and you do the clavicle cautery according to the shape described above.
de la marris	of the wound
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the mare is cold and moist, and does not allow him to conceive, and the flowers are rotten and late in appearing; and when they come, so great a pain do they cause: then it is necessary that he make three cauterizations around the belly, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the back; and let the cauterization be clamped, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip socket, and for this reason he moves out of his place, and the sign is that the leg is longer than the other when measured together; and the joints are found to be sore, then you should make a circle-like cauterization on the hip socket, and mark in front of the joint around the socket as she turns, so that the socket is within the circle; and if it is, make the cauterization such as those with which we have cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this fire cautery is not present, make three cauteries with the olive oil, and let the cauteries be complete as well; and treat it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then it is appropriate that you purge the patient of large humors with foul pills, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After this, make the cautery; and the manner of the cautery should be according to two manners: that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery is according to many manners, of which one is this: that you cauterize over the hip joint three triangular cauteries according to this form, and make them deep and wide, and between each cautery have the size of two, and let the olive oil cautery be; never do a cautery in the middle on top of the head of the hip, for there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that the fire cautery at the circle that we have just said in the dislocation of the hip; but do it in such a way that the circles contain all the hip, and all the flesh of the body is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way that is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make II fire cauteries there where the patient says that the pain is, and a cautery above the ankle three times, two on the left side; and either make the cauterization scalpel-like, or burn the thickness of the flesh; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two toes or near it, make the fire cautery there, which is called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if he is a physician, let him do more; and if he feels that the pain is in the knee joint towards the thigh, let him perform cauterization with the knife or circular cautery, and let you take good care of all your cauteries so that you do not leave them for even a moment, while burning the nerves and large arteries, and causing more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have also seen many who have performed cauterization on the foot's heel, and left it for so long that the leg was completely collapsed, and the bones as well, and became pierced and rotten in all the bones.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a treatment for the belly that caused death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, perform cauterization on one and then on the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise men said in the cauterization of the ankle, for this is the manner, make one so large and thick as a thumb nail, or a little less, and between the two cheeks be of the quantity of a pea's width; and let the cheeks be higher on either side, and also as long as fingers, and all of good iron; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be heated until it is entirely red and hot, and then put it on the box of the sick hip, and let it turn to the right side; and let one cauterize him once and let him rest for three days; and then make a poultice with butter, and leave the wound open for a long time; after the cure of ointment until he is well.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Al-Buqaqum says that we use little of this cautery because of the danger of its regurgitation, and few use it; however, this is a good cautery that can endure it, and let it be applied where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The medical cautery of fiery tools is so that you make an instrument with a handle on one end and another on the other, and let it be of brass or iron with a wall at a distance, and at its height there are two holes, each of which has the thickness of a thumb; and they open from top to bottom and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After laying him down on his back with his head at the foot of the bed and his chest supported by a pillow, you will then place your hand very high up on his thigh; after that, you will cut off two circles from the warm awl that has been heated in the fire for one hour, and let them cool for a while, so that they can cause the patient pain and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is true that these also cause a stinging sensation like fire; and when the stinging has passed, you will remove your hand from the instrument and lower the leg of warm wool, and leave it there for three days, and place it in vinegar until the blackening is removed; and let it be for three days until the pus forms; and he would receive help behind after the treatment with ointments until he is well.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, you will make a warm awl in the same way that you did for the hainche; and this is the method of the hot awl, and I have written it down here in the treatise on medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together and put them in a nine-pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Take some small holes so that the point of a razor can enter; and place that pot on top of another well-plumbed pot, and put alkali and charcoal and water softener on it, so much as to cover both the powders completely - you will have to hold them tightly in your hand; and leave them like that until they are all dry and crack; then take all of that water, and pour it over the charcoal and alkali, just as you did before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then if it is very dry and is used up in the work of medicine and other treatments; because it does this work like fire, and with other medicines that are well-mixed together: honey, mustard, and charcoal with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galien tells us of a cure in which an honorable person was cured of the pain of the hip and sciatic vein, and he soaked himself, and he said that no other cure was made, and he was healed at once when this cure was done, and he bathed himself as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he said in this way that you grind green fresh tar and dry it up, and mix it with a little fat, and put it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and let it sit; and leave it for three hours, and because of the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then he makes him enter or bathe until his body is slightly warm, and he makes him enter the bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery with these medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with the ends of a deer's horn, then it heals well; and the cauterization must be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another, and wipe it with oil; and put it on the fissure which is between the thumb and the finger called the index.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Afterwards take dry ends of a deer's horn, and hold them over a fire until they are charred, and put them on the wool, and leave them there until they are blackened; then repeat it, doing so as long as you think that it is coming to the hip, and the pain is ceasing; and this way of cauterizing is called "deer horn cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of the back pain
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or through eating too much, or through excessive evaporation, or through the appearance of expanded cold matter, there are no remedies for these, except that the one who comes from the infusion of cold matter should be treated.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	He must then give him the pills of rot or other, which cause pain in his loins, three lines signed by inch, and in each line five cauterizations or more according to the usefulness and the quantity that the sick can support; and it is done cauterization according to the cauterization called "point"; and if you see, make three cauterizations or four at the clavicle-like cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often affects small children, and the signs of the beginning are that they become stiff when they stand up and fear; and you see in the last spine of the back and in us the appearance that comes on the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see him cured, let him be cauterized with the clavicle-like cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	Let the fire cautery equally affect each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you can see, cauterize evenly around the spine with the fire cautery, keeping the points of the burning tool about two or three lines apart, and let them be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the fire cautery has been applied, as we have described, take care not to apply it to the gizzards in such a way that it reaches the nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	that cause pain in the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the joints ache because of moisture that spreads to each limb, and when pain comes from the foot, what is known properly as podagra, and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured with medicine, then cure it with fire cautery in this way: Make the fire cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-colored according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary that you touch on the face of the foot, make a fire cautery to all the fire cauteries that are claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come only up to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, do a fire cautery on each knee III cauterizes or IV of each part, in all olive cauterize; and if you need more, do more, but don't hold your hand tight except for as long as the skin of the leg is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains go down to the knees and back, administer the cautery that we have spoken of in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, do two lines of fire; and if there is no pain left in the two, do a fire cautery on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come only up to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good advice to the patient and use medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you do this good government and you purge the wind, then you will be healed by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the syph
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes in the groin, and the ball becomes hot and new, then it is necessary that when you see him heal, he does not eat meat that day; and use things that cool his belly, so that the end sinks from his belly; then let him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to shave his beard as long as his balls are repaired, and bring them to your hands, and sign by cutting above the bone of the testicle, and all a sign that is like half a circle above the neck; then heat the fire with which it is done:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as he is white and has a pleasant smell.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then return the balls to their place; and the minister should hold his hand so that it does not turn back; and work well on the legs of the sick person, and put a pair of shoes on him and a sergeant on his legs, and another on his feet which hold his hands; then place the cauterizer on his sign on all your hand, and hold it straight and hold it as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not hit it the first time, start again another time until you come to the bone; and guard carefully that the ball does not move when you are making the cauterization; that you do not burn it; and that by this the sick person does not die, or any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you come to the bone with the cauterizer, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterizer of children be subtle according to their size, and of big people also great according to their size; after III days cure the place of the cauterizer of butter until the scorching is healed; after it cure other ointments until it is healthy, and lay the sick person for 40 days on his back until the wound is well fixed; and it is necessary that his bandages be loosened slowly, so that the ball does not come out when he goes to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, they bring him a well-made bandage, and change it every 40 days; and let there be good rest, that he works little and guards against too much drinking and eating, and against too much yelling; and when he does this teaching then is he entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say here the cure of cauterizing in his ointment.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture from the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, they do the cauterization of the cauterization according to its quantity, and let it be burned on the third cure; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the old ones said that one should cauterize with the cauterizer at III angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the head of the neck; and make a line with your finger across the wound from side to side, and another behind it, and hold all the nail clippings together in your hand.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterization is lighter and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	causing old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any limb, or from a bruise or an injury, and this pain continues for a long time, and the medical cure does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize with the fire that is called "pinceau", and do the cauterization according to the length of the limb, its smallness and weakness, and its virtue and location of torments and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If he is well after the first cauterization, it is good; but if not, start again with another cauterization on top of that one, for this is the custom: you must keep applying the cauterizations until the patient is completely healed.
de meselerie	of medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Of disease, are treated once with cauterization by great help, and most often by the disease that comes from the putrefaction of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you can see the cauterizer, take care that the disease is at the beginning, and if it is cured according to what we said in the division of diseases, and does not rest or remain, and you doubt that corruption will pervade the whole malady, then you shall do V cauterizes on the top of the head: I cut off the top, and the other towards the front at the end of the hair; and II on the two horns, and I behind on the nape; and I let it burn so long with the cauterizer that it comes to the bone, and so long that the scabs come out without any vapors of bad humors coming out; then cauterize the mouse according to what it is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	Et si le malade a la fièvre, il faut lui faire une cautérisation avec du feu sur tout son corps; et si la fièvre baisse, alors il faut faire des cautères comme ceux-ci: un cautère sur la nuque, deux sur l'arrière du cou, six sur le dos, un grand sur la tête, un autre petit près de l'ombilic, deux sur les épaules, deux sur les côtes, un sur chaque joint des mains et des pieds, et un dans la paume de la main. Il faut aussi se méfier des nerfs qui courent sous le corps et qu'il ne faut pas brûler; et il ne faut jamais faire de cautère sur l'os du poignet ou sur celui de l'estomac, ni sur le foie.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And if the patient has a fever, then he must have his whole body cauterized with fire; and if the fever goes down, then you must make the following types of cauterization: one on the neck, two on the back of the neck, six on the back, one large on the head, one small near the navel, two on the shoulders, two on the ribs, one on each joint of the hands and feet, and one in the palm of the hand. You must also be careful of the nerves that run under the body and not to burn them; and you should never make a cauterization on the wrist bone or on the stomach bone, nor on the liver. And know that when I do more cauterizations, then I do more help and benefit; and know that the patient does not feel pain from the cauterization as much as the healthy person feels it, because the body is already very corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization is great and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in iron ways.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the cure, leave the wound of flour with honey and other cures until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the swelling comes to any member and is cured with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healthy, then make the cauterization on the member according to its greatness and smallness; and let the cauterization be a little entering into the flesh of the cure; and then heal with ointments until it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And no time is made to cauterize and by hand and by foot and at the back, at the exit of the nerve that silences the member, and thus if it is osteoclast; but nevertheless do not interfere with it unless you know the members and exits of moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	of the back
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the patient called "albaras" is awake and the medicine does not help, then burn him with a fire cautery very slightly, according to the quantity of the juice of curcuma, until the blenchour [a type of fever] is taken out and its color changes; then treat with flour of barley and lentils with oil of roses and leaves of plantain, and blood of lamb and blood of owl, each in part; and mix them all together, and bind them with a cloth, and apply it to the fire until he is cured.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment for syphilis by fire cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the plague [syphilis] begins to appear, and you see it stopping, then burn it with a fire cautery that seems like a circle all around the area of the plague.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And some say that one should also burn the center of the plague; but I do not think this is good, for it will reduce it to a ulcer and corruption, and I have never heard of such a thing; and it is even better to burn around it with the fire cautery we call 'circular', as we have said in many a cauterization.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the inflammation that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it takes a long time to die, or because of the waste the disease produces, or because the patient is very old and weak and has little blood, or because they are very young; then you should hasten their death: therefore cauterize them with a little fire by poking them with it; after that leave them alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For they will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you pierce them all over with the fire, then heat the fire in this way:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of the disease called "adubelati" as long as the fire has penetrated the flesh, and make the burns so that the patient feels the heat in one way and the course of putrefaction is stopped in another way.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment as long as he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	with fire,
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of getting sick, which is called "corrosion," and is nothing more than a certain type of wound, as the fire dries up the members just as it does with dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in a person who can be treated, then you should heat the clavy cauterizes, small and large, according to what is appropriate for the place where the disease is; after the fire has completely burned away all corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupt is bone.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days and put clavy cauterizes on the affected areas to keep them oiled until the burns from the fire are healed, and all corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment with the oil that causes blisters:
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that there is no healing, it is good; and if not, then begin again the cauterization on that which has been delayed from its place corrupt.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this mengeson is never once cured of the medical fever by the fire cautery; but yet the fire cautery is of more great help, and I have already said the cure of the medical fever in the division: take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the onions that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	At times it happens that by accident a disease called "close" according to our intention comes about, and it is a big thing that hurts the foot.

C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say fire cauterization, and cauterization by hot water.

li cure dou trembler	to shake off

quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut off
